  711   
  712   static const mxArray *c_emlrt_marshallOut(const b_struct_T *u)
  713   {
  714     const mxArray *b_y;
  715     const mxArray *c_y;
  716     static const int32_T iv59[1] = { 15 };
  717   
  718     const mxArray *m24;
  719     real_T (*pData)[];
  720     int32_T i;
  721     const mxArray *d_y;
  722     static const int32_T iv60[2] = { 48, 12 };
  723   
  724     creal_T b_u[576];
  725     const mxArray *e_y;
  726     static const int32_T iv61[1] = { 53 };
  727   
  728     creal_T c_u[53];
  729     const mxArray *f_y;
  730     static const int32_T iv62[1] = { 80 };
  731   
  732     const mxArray *g_y;
  733     b_y = NULL;
  734     emlrtAssign(&b_y, mxCreateStructMatrix(1, 1, 0, NULL));
  735     emlrtAddField(b_y, emlrt_marshallOut(u->phi), "phi", 0);
  736     emlrtAddField(b_y, emlrt_marshallOut(u->delay), "delay", 0);
  737     emlrtAddField(b_y, emlrt_marshallOut(u->numPeaks), "numPeaks", 0);
  738     c_y = NULL;
  739     m24 = mxCreateNumericArray(1, (int32_T *)&iv59, mxDOUBLE_CLASS, mxREAL);
  740     pData = (real_T (*)[])mxGetPr(m24);
  741     for (i = 0; i < 15; i++) {
  742       (*pData)[i] = u->frequency[i];
  743     }
  744   
  745     emlrtAssign(&c_y, m24);
  746     emlrtAddField(b_y, c_y, "frequency", 0);
  747     emlrtAddField(b_y, emlrt_marshallOut(u->phase), "phase", 0);
  748     emlrtAddField(b_y, emlrt_marshallOut(u->frequencyMA), "frequencyMA", 0);
  749     emlrtAddField(b_y, emlrt_marshallOut(u->numProcessed), "numProcessed", 0);
  750     emlrtAddField(b_y, emlrt_marshallOut(u->inputBufferLength),
  751                   "inputBufferLength", 0);
  752     emlrtAddField(b_y, emlrt_marshallOut(u->numFreqToAverage), "numFreqToAverage",
  753                   0);
  754     d_y = NULL;
  755     m24 = mxCreateNumericArray(2, (int32_T *)&iv60, mxDOUBLE_CLASS, mxCOMPLEX);
  756     for (i = 0; i < 576; i++) {
  757       b_u[i] = u->pilotEqGains[i];
  758     }
  759   
  760     emlrtExportNumericArrayR2013a(emlrtRootTLSGlobal, m24, b_u, 8);
  761     emlrtAssign(&d_y, m24);
  762     emlrtAddField(b_y, d_y, "pilotEqGains", 0);
  763     e_y = NULL;
  764     m24 = mxCreateNumericArray(1, (int32_T *)&iv61, mxDOUBLE_CLASS, mxCOMPLEX);
  765     for (i = 0; i < 53; i++) {
  766       c_u[i] = u->preambleEqGains[i];
  767     }
  768   
  769     emlrtExportNumericArrayR2013a(emlrtRootTLSGlobal, m24, c_u, 8);
  770     emlrtAssign(&e_y, m24);
  771     emlrtAddField(b_y, e_y, "preambleEqGains", 0);
  772     f_y = NULL;
  773     m24 = mxCreateNumericArray(1, (int32_T *)&iv62, mxDOUBLE_CLASS, mxREAL);
  774     pData = (real_T (*)[])mxGetPr(m24);
  775     for (i = 0; i < 80; i++) {
  776       (*pData)[i] = u->message[i];
  777     }
  778   
  779     emlrtAssign(&f_y, m24);
  780     emlrtAddField(b_y, f_y, "message", 0);
  781     g_y = NULL;
  782     m24 = mxCreateLogicalScalar(u->printReceivedData);
  783     emlrtAssign(&g_y, m24);
  784     emlrtAddField(b_y, g_y, "printReceivedData", 0);
  785     return b_y;
  786   }
